350  set GetPricesFirst;
351  MarketCap=close*BSSharesOutCommon;
352  EarningsYield=  EBIT / (MarketCap + BSTotalCurrentLiabilities + BSLTDebt + BSMinorIntLiab +
352! BSPrefStockEq - BSCash);
353  run;
